# -*- ck2.events -*-

namespace = emf_nomad

# emf_nomad.1000
#
# Invoked on startup to build temples & tribes as necessary to preserve
# the culture+religion, as specified in province history, of each potentially
# nomad-affected province on the map at any playable start date. Each
# such province is given its own province_event, the ID of which is
# 1000 + <province ID> in this namespace.
#
# NOTE: None of these province events actually execute unless they are
# actually found to be empty/nomadic at runtime, so while there may be
# a lot of events here, an extremely tiny portion of the events will run at
# any given start.
#
# How these events were created: All event code following was generated
# automatically by a program which emulates CK2 history execution, written
# by a secret ninja order. If in need, contact zijistark (azrinon@gmail.com)
# so that he may relay your message to said ninjas and deliver their reply.

# emf_nomad.1400 [400 - Zyriane]
province_event = {
	id = emf_nomad.1400

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = { is_nomadic = yes }
		NOT = { any_province_holding = { NOT = { holding_type = nomad } } }
		has_empty_holding = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { culture = samoyed religion = finnish_pagan }
			break = yes # Not necessary to build a settlement
		}
		build_holding = { type = tribal }
		culture  = samoyed
		religion = finnish_pagan
		emf_nomad_antinomad_tribal = yes
		log = "emf_antinomad(400, '[Root.GetName]') => tribal / samoyed / finnish_pagan"
	}
}

		owner = { is_nomadic = yes }
		NOT = { any_province_holding = { NOT = { holding_type = nomad } } }
		has_empty_holding = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { culture = crimean_gothic religion = orthodox }
			break = yes # Not necessary to build a settlement
		}
		build_holding = { type = temple }
		culture  = crimean_gothic
		religion = orthodox
		emf_nomad_antinomad_temple = yes
		log = "emf_antinomad(562, '[Root.GetName]') => temple / crimean_gothic / orthodox"
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = { is_nomadic = yes }
		NOT = { any_province_holding = { NOT = { holding_type = nomad } } }
		has_empty_holding = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { culture = mordvin religion = finnish_pagan }
			break = yes # Not necessary to build a settlement
		}
		build_holding = { type = temple }
		culture  = mordvin
		religion = finnish_pagan
		emf_nomad_antinomad_temple = yes
		log = "emf_antinomad(588, '[Root.GetName]') => temple / mordvin / finnish_pagan"
	}
}

			break = yes # Not necessary to build a settlement
		}
		build_holding = { type = tribal }
		culture  = mongol
		religion = sunni
		emf_nomad_antinomad_tribal = yes
		log = "emf_antinomad(617, '[Root.GetName]') => tribal / mongol / sunni"
	}
}

	immediate = {

				break = yes # Not necessary to build a settlement
			}

			culture  = meshchera
			religion = finnish_pagan
			emf_nomad_antinomad_tribal = yes
			log = "emf_antinomad(1669, '[Root.GetName]') => tribal / meshchera / finnish_pagan"

		religion = tengri_pagan

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = { is_nomadic = yes }
		NOT = { any_province_holding = { NOT = { holding_type = nomad } } }
		has_empty_holding = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { year = 1227 } }
			if = {
				limit = { culture = uyghur religion = tengri_pagan }
				break = yes # Not necessary to build a settlement
			}
			build_holding = { type = tribal }
			culture  = uyghur
			religion = tengri_pagan
